GT Equivalence Verification (BPG2)
============================================================
GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*P*exp(-c3*t)
Candidate formulas: 53

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(t,P)=P\Big(0.2569297861\,\sin(0.7218439643\,t)+0.1149290460\,e^{-0.03038461977\,t}\Big).
\]
So any matching candidate must be **linear in \(P\)** (no \(\sqrt P\), \(P^2\), \(|P|\), \(\log(P\cdot)\), etc.), must have **exactly** a \(P\sin(\alpha t)\) term (no phase shift unless it can be removed), and a **\(P e^{\beta t}\)** term with \(\beta<0\), and **no extra \(t\)-only or \(P\)-only additive terms**.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether all “extra” structures can be zeroed out and whether the remaining structure can be parameter-set to the GT.

---

### 1. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\sqrt t+c4\log(Pc5+1)+c6 e^{c7 t}\log(Pc8+1)\)
Can set \(c3=c4=c6=0\) to remove extra terms. Left with \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)\) only, missing the required \(P e^{-0.0303 t}\) term. **No.**

### 2. \(\sqrt P c0 + P c1\sin(c2 t+c3)+c4 e^{c5 t}\log(Pc6+1)\)
Set \(c0=0\), \(c4=0\) leaves \(P c1\sin(c2 t+c3)\) only; still missing exponential term. Also phase shift issue. **No.**

### 3. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\log(Pc4+1)+c5 \frac{t}{c6+t}+c7 e^{c8 t}\log(Pc9+1)\)
Zero out extras: \(c3=c5=c7=0\) leaves only sine term; missing exponential. **No.**

### 4. \(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2+c1}+P c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+c5\log(Pc6+1)+c7 e^{c8 t}\log(Pc9+1)\)
To match GT must be linear in \(P\). The rational \(P^2/(P^2+c1)\) cannot become \(P\) for all \(P\); best is kill it with \(c0=0\). Also kill logs: \(c5=c7=0\). Left with sine only; missing exponential. **No.**

### 5. \(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2+c1}+P c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+c5+c6 e^{c7 t}\log(Pc8+1)\)
Kill rational \(c0=0\), kill constant \(c5=0\), kill log term \(c6=0\). Left with sine only. **No.**

### 6. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\log(Pc4+1)+c5 t^{c6} e^{c7 t}\log(Pc8+1)\)
Kill log terms \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\) leaves sine only. **No.**

### 7. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\log(Pc4+1)+\frac{c5}{c6+t}+c7 e^{c8 t}\log(Pc9+1)\)
Set \(c3=c5=c7=0\) leaves sine only. **No.**

### 8. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 e^{P c4}+c5 e^{c6 t}\log(Pc7+1)\)
Need no \(e^{P c4}\) term ⇒ set \(c3=0\). Need no log term ⇒ set \(c5=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 9. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\log(Pc4+1)+c5 e^{c6 t}\log(Pc7+1)\)
Kill log terms \(c3=0,c5=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 10. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 e^{c5|P|}+c6 e^{c7 t}\log(c8|P|+1)\)
Must remove \(P\)-nonlinear terms: set \(c4=0,c6=0\). Also constant \(c3=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 11. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 t+c4 e^{c5 t}\log(Pc6+1)\)
Kill \(c3=0\), kill log term \(c4=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 12. \(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2+c1}+P c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+c5 e^{c6 t}|P|^{c7}\)
To be linear in \(P\), the \(|P|^{c7}\) term would need to become \(P\) for all real \(P\), impossible (absolute value). Best kill it \(c5=0\). Kill rational \(c0=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 13. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5 t\)
Kill \(c5=0\). Then we have exactly \(P(\text{sine}+\text{exponential})\), which matches GT form **if** we can remove phase shift \(c2\).
- GT has \(\sin(0.7218 t)\) with **no phase**. Candidate has \(\sin(c1 t+c2)\). For equality for all \(t\), must have \(c2=0\) (or \(2\pi k\), which is equivalent).
Then set:
- \(c0=0.2569297861044923\)
- \(c1=0.7218439642922193\)
- \(c3=0.11492904603507054\)
- \(c4=-0.030384619767814418\)
This yields exact GT. **Yes, matches.**

### 14. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}\)
Same reasoning as 13 but without needing to kill \(c5 t\). Require \(c2=0\) (mod \(2\pi\)), then choose:
- \(c0=0.2569297861044923\)
- \(c1=0.7218439642922193\)
- \(c3=0.11492904603507054\)
- \(c4=-0.030384619767814418\)
Gives GT exactly. **Yes, matches.**

### 15. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 e^{c4 t}|P|\)
\(|P|\) cannot equal \(P\) for all real \(P\). If restrict to \(P\ge 0\) it could, but problem is “all values” (implicitly real). Only way is set \(c3=0\), leaving sine only. **No.**

### 16. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P\frac{c3}{P+c4}+P^{c5} c6 e^{c7 t}\)
The \(P\frac{c3}{P+c4}\) term cannot be made identically 0 unless \(c3=0\). Then we need \(P^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}\) to become \(P\cdot(\text{const})e^{\beta t}\): set \(c5=1\). That would give correct \(P e^{c7 t}\) term. But we still must handle sine phase \(c2=0\). So with \(c3=0,c5=1,c2=0\), it *could* match GT by setting \(c0,c1,c6,c7\) appropriately. However note: then candidate becomes \(P c0\sin(c1 t)+P c6 e^{c7 t}\), which is exactly GT form. So **Yes, matches** (choose \(c6=0.114929...\), \(c7=-0.0303846...\), etc.).

### 17. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\log(Pc6+1)\)
Must remove log term: \(c5=0\). Then identical to candidate 14; require \(c2=0\) and set remaining constants to GT. **Yes, matches.**

### 18. \(\sqrt P c0 + P c1\sin(c2 t+c3)+P c4 e^{c5 t}\)
Kill \(\sqrt P\) term: \(c0=0\). Then we have \(P(\sin(\cdot)+e^{\cdot})\). Need \(c3=0\) to remove phase shift. Then set \(c1,c2,c4,c5\) to GT values. **Yes, matches.**

### 19. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\cos(c6 t+c7)\)
Extra cosine term must vanish: \(c5=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 20. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P c1\sin(c2 t+c3)+P^{c4}c5 e^{c6 t}\)
Need no \(P^{1/3}\) term ⇒ \(c0=0\). Need exponential term linear in \(P\) ⇒ set \(c4=1\). Need sine phase \(c3=0\). Then matches GT by setting \(c1,c2,c5,c6\). **Yes, matches.**

### 21. \(P^{1/3}c0 + P c1\sin(c2 t+c3)+P c4 e^{c5 t}\)
Set \(c0=0\), set \(c3=0\), then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 22. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}\sin(c5 t+c6)+c7 e^{c8 t}+c9\)
To remove non-GT terms: need \(c7=0,c9=0\). The middle term is \(P e^{c4 t}\sin(\cdot)\), not a pure exponential; cannot become pure exponential for all \(t\) unless amplitude 0 ⇒ \(c3=0\). Then left sine only. **No.**

### 23. \(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2+c1}+P c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+c5 e^{c6 t}|P|^{c7}\)
As in 12: \(|P|^{c7}\) can’t become \(P\) for all real \(P\); kill \(c5=0\). Kill rational \(c0=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 24. \(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2+c1}+P c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+P^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}+c8\log(Pc9+1)\)
Kill rational \(c0=0\). Kill log \(c8=0\). Set \(c5=1\) to get linear \(P\) exponential term. Require sine phase \(c4=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 25. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t)+\frac{c5}{P^2+c6}+c7\)
Extra \(P\)-rational term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c7=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 26. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 e^{c5 t}|P|\)
\(|P|\) issue: cannot equal \(P\) for all real \(P\). Only option kill exponential term \(c4=0\) and constant \(c3=0\), leaving sine only. **No.**

### 27. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\)
Set \(c5=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 28. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}+c6 e^{P c7}\)
Must kill \(e^{P c7}\): set \(c6=0\). Need \(P^{c3}\) to be \(P\): set \(c3=1\). Need phase \(c2=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 29. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}+\frac{c6}{P^2+c7}+c8\)
Kill rational term \(c6=0\), kill constant \(c8=0\). Set \(c3=1\). Require \(c2=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 30. \(P c0\sin(c1+c2 t)+c3 e^{c4 t}\sin(P c5+c6)\)
Second term depends on \(P\) inside sine; GT has no such dependence. Must set \(c3=0\), leaving \(P c0\sin(c1+c2 t)\). This can match the sine part (set \(c1=0,c2=0.7218,c0=0.2569\)) but missing exponential term. **No.**

### 31. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\log(Pc6+1)+c7 \frac{t}{c8+t}\)
Kill log \(c5=0\), kill rational-in-t \(c7=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 32. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}\cos(c5 t+c6)+c7\cos(c8 t+c9)\)
To remove last cosine: \(c7=0\). Middle term is exponential times cosine; cannot become pure exponential unless \(c3=0\) (or cosine constant 1 for all t, impossible unless frequency 0 and phase 0: set \(c5=0\) gives \(\cos(c6)\) constant; then it *can* be absorbed into coefficient). Indeed set \(c5=0\) so \(\cos(c6)\) is constant; then term becomes \(P(c3\cos(c6))e^{c4 t}\), a pure exponential. Then require \(c2=0\). Choose \(c3\cos(c6)=0.114929...\) (possible by picking \(c6=0\) and \(c3\) accordingly). **Yes, matches.**

### 33. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\sqrt t+c6\log(Pc7+1)\)
Kill \(c5=0,c6=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 34. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 e^{c5 t}\sin(P c6+c7)\)
The \(e^{c5 t}\sin(Pc6+c7)\) depends on \(P\) nonlinearly; must set \(c4=0\). Also \(c3=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 35. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5 t e^{c6 t}\)
Extra \(t e^{c6 t}\) must vanish: \(c5=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 36. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5 e^{c6 t}+c7\)
Extra term \(c5 e^{c6 t}\) is not multiplied by \(P\); must set \(c5=0\). Also constant \(c7=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 37. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}+c6\log(Pc7+1)+c8 \frac{t}{c9+t}\)
Kill log \(c6=0\), kill rational-in-t \(c8=0\). Set \(c3=1\). Require \(c2=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 38. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}+c6\log(Pc7+1)+\frac{c8}{c9+t}\)
Kill log \(c6=0\), kill \(\frac{c8}{c9+t}\) via \(c8=0\). Set \(c3=1\). Require \(c2=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 39. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}\sin(c6 t+c7)+c8 t\)
Need remove \(c8 t\): set \(c8=0\). The exponential term has extra \(\sin(c6 t+c7)\); can make it constant by setting \(c6=0\), giving \(\sin(c7)\) constant, so term becomes \(P^{c3}(c4\sin c7)e^{c5 t}\). Then set \(c3=1\). Require \(c2=0\). Then match constants (choose \(c7=\pi/2\) so \(\sin c7=1\)). **Yes, matches.**

### 40. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P\frac{c3}{P+c4}+P^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}\sin(c8 t+c9)\)
Kill rational-in-P term: \(c3=0\). Exponential has extra sine; make constant by \(c8=0\) so \(\sin(c9)\) constant. Then set \(c5=1\). Require \(c2=0\). Then match constants (pick \(c9=\pi/2\)). **Yes, matches.**

### 41. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5 e^{P c6}+c7 \frac{t}{c8+t}\)
Kill \(e^{P c6}\): \(c5=0\). Kill rational-in-t: \(c7=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 42. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5 e^{c6 t}\)
Extra \(c5 e^{c6 t}\) not multiplied by \(P\); must set \(c5=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 43. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P c3 e^{c4 t}+c5\log(c6 t+1)+c7 e^{c8 t}\)
Extra \(\log(c6 t+1)\) must vanish: \(c5=0\). Extra \(c7 e^{c8 t}\) must vanish: \(c7=0\). Then same as 14; require \(c2=0\). **Yes, matches.**

### 44. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P\frac{c3}{P+c4}+P^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}+c8 e^{c9 t}\)
Kill rational-in-P: \(c3=0\). Kill extra non-\(P\) exponential: \(c8=0\). Set \(c5=1\). Require \(c2=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 45. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}+c6 e^{P c7}+c8\)
Kill \(e^{P c7}\): \(c6=0\). Kill constant \(c8=0\). Set \(c3=1\). Require \(c2=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 46. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 e^{c5|P|}+c6 e^{c7 t}|P|^{c8}\)
Absolute value prevents matching linear \(P\) dependence for all real \(P\). Must set \(c4=0\) and \(c6=0\), and \(c3=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 47. \(P^2 c0 + P c1 + P c2\sin(c3 t+c4)+P^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}+c8 t+c9\)
Must remove \(P^2\) term: \(c0=0\). Remove linear-in-P constant term \(P c1\): set \(c1=0\). Remove \(c8 t\): \(c8=0\). Remove constant \(c9=0\). Set \(c5=1\). Require sine phase \(c4=0\). Then remaining is \(P c2\sin(c3 t)+P c6 e^{c7 t}\), match GT by setting constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 48. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 t e^{c4 t}+c5 e^{c6 t}|P|^{c7}\)
\(|P|^{c7}\) cannot become \(P\) for all real \(P\); kill \(c5=0\). Also must kill \(c3 t e^{c4 t}\) via \(c3=0\). Left sine only. **No.**

### 49. \(\sqrt P c0\log(c1 t+1)\cos(c2 t+c3)+P c4\sin(c5 t+c6)+P c7 e^{c8 t}\)
First term must vanish: \(c0=0\). Then we have \(P c4\sin(c5 t+c6)+P c7 e^{c8 t}\). Require \(c6=0\) to remove phase shift. Then set \(c4,c5,c7,c8\) to GT constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 50. \(\sqrt P c0\log(c1 t+1)\cos(c2 t+c3)+P c4\sin(c5 t+c6)+c7 e^{c8 t}\log(Pc9+1)\)
Kill first term \(c0=0\). Kill log-in-P term \(c7=0\). Left only sine term; missing exponential. **No.**

### 51. \(P c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+P^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}+c6 e^{c7 t}\)
Extra \(c6 e^{c7 t}\) not multiplied by \(P\); must set \(c6=0\). Then set \(c3=1\), require \(c2=0\), and match constants. **Yes, matches.**

### 52. \(\sqrt P c0\cos(c1 t+c2)+P c3\sin(c4 t+c5)+c6 e^{c7 t}\log(Pc8+1)\)
Kill \(\sqrt P\) term: \(c0=0\). Kill log term: \(c6=0\). Left sine only; missing exponential. **No.**

### 53. \(P^{1/3}c0+P c1\sin(c2 t+c3)+P c4 e^{c5 t}+c6\sin(c7 t+c8)\)
Kill \(P^{1/3}\) term: \(c0=0\). Kill extra sine not multiplied by \(P\): \(c6=0\). Require \(c3=0\). Then match constants. **Yes, matches.**
